bothe father ruler yee goddes fyre swoord gaue way tyme yee aenaeas came troy yee goddes mortall men canonyzed thou qui whoo didst reere walles roome mar whoo wart valcant quirins syre vesta household goddes caesar thy fyre holy thou phebus whoo vesta also art household thou iupiter whoo hyghest part mountayne tarpey haste thy church yee goddes may conscience sauf poet bee appealed pray let day bee slowe comme dead augustus whoo world head quyght giuing vp care therof ascend heauen ay absent hence fauour vntoo shall pray haue brought woork end neither ioues feerce wrath swoord fyre freating age
